\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmmgs__tools_8c_source_l01194}01194   \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} tensordot[3];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmmgs__tools_8c_source_l01195}01195   tensordot[0] = 0.;}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmmgs__tools_8c_source_l01199}01199   \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} ( j=0; j<ilist; ++j ) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmmgs__tools_8c_source_l01200}01200     \textcolor{comment}{/* Compute the 2D metric tensor from the projection of the vectors on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmmgs__tools_8c_source_l01201}01201 \textcolor{comment}{     * the tangent plane */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmmgs__tools_8c_source_l01202}01202     tensordot[0] += lispoi[3*j+1]*lispoi[3*j+1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmmgs__tools_8c_source_l01203}01203     tensordot[1] += lispoi[3*j+1]*lispoi[3*j+2];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmmgs__tools_8c_source_l01204}01204     tensordot[2] += lispoi[3*j+2]*lispoi[3*j+2];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmmgs__tools_8c_source_l01205}01205   \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmmgs__tools_8c_source_l01206}01206 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmmgs__tools_8c_source_l01207}01207   \textcolor{comment}{/* Metric = nedges/dim * inv (sum(tensor\_dot(edges,edges)))  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmmgs__tools_8c_source_l01208}01208   dd = 1./(tensordot[0]*tensordot[2] -\/ tensordot[1]*tensordot[1]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmmgs__tools_8c_source_l01209}01209   dd *= (double)ilist/2.;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmmgs__tools_8c_source_l01210}01210 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmmgs__tools_8c_source_l01211}01211   \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} \mbox{\hyperlink{API__functionsf__2d_8c_a5be62287edda5e00fb0cde8ab34e70c5}{tmp}} = tensordot[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmmgs__tools_8c_source_l01212}01212 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmmgs__tools_8c_source_l01213}01213   tensordot[0] = dd*tensordot[2];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmmgs__tools_8c_source_l01214}01214   tensordot[1] = -\/dd*tensordot[1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmmgs__tools_8c_source_l01215}01215   tensordot[2] = dd*\mbox{\hyperlink{API__functionsf__2d_8c_a5be62287edda5e00fb0cde8ab34e70c5}{tmp}};}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmmgs__tools_8c_source_l01229}01229   \textcolor{comment}{/* At this point, tensordot (with 0 replaced by isqhmax in the z}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmmgs__tools_8c_source_l01230}01230 \textcolor{comment}{     direction) is the desired metric, except it is expressed in the rotated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmmgs__tools_8c_source_l01231}01231 \textcolor{comment}{     canonical basis, that is tensordot = R * metric in cb * \string^t R, so metric}}
